       <h2>
        Welcome to Copper River Cabinet Company of Fort Wayne and Warsaw, Indiana.
       </h2>
       <p>
        While there may be hundreds, even thousands of other cabinet stores, there has never been a place quite like Copper River. It’s a place where you will find the finest in cabinets and much more for your home. A company led by the motto “Give your customers more than they expect at a price they can afford.
       </p>
